<L.6.1>
<Z>Version 4.2 Update <C> You'll notice (hopefully) that the software is now flagged as version 4.2, and an update is included<L.31.1>
this time (or for those who receive results via email, it's on www.pbmsports.com via the Developments link).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
The changes are all fairly minor - it's basically three things:-<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
1. The extra Pinch Hitting positions previously detailed:- MIF, CIF and COF.<L.31.1>
2. The first round playoff series are now played over a 2-2-1 format, not the old 2-3 format.<L.31.1>
3. The wild card team is now always seeded 4, and cannot play a divisional rival in the first round.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
The latter two are fairly cosmetic, but mirror real-life. In both cases they won't apply to seasons already running, so when you<L.31.1>
move to a new season you'll see the software flag your game as "2005 rules". The 2-2-1 format has one real impact, and one<L.31.1>
"perceived impact". The perceived impact is that the higher seed now starts the series at home, but this really is only<L.31.1>
psychological (and isn't built into Gameplan Baseball) but it does now have an extra travel day factored in, so teams get a day's<L.31.1>
rest after game 4, and it does give you even more scope for playing with a "short rotation" (hence I think it's unfair to<L.31.1>
introduce it midseason). This argument also applies to the seeding thing, which is utterly sensible. A wild card team shouldn't be<L.31.1>
seeded above a divisional winner, and now as in real-life, two divisional rivals cannot meet in the first round.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Version 4.2 Rules <C> There are now two formats to the Version 4.2 rulebook. One is the Version 3.1 printed rulebook (I still<L.31.1>
have a stack of these, so I'll keep using them until they've all done) combined with the version 4.2 update, but I've also (with<L.31.1>
thanks to Paul Maguire) got a PDF format of the two combined (ie the extra paragraphs are incorporated into the full rulebook)<L.31.1>
which you can download from www.pbmsports.com - if you don't have access to the internet don't worry, you aren't missing anything<L.31.1>
- it's all combined in the 3.1 rulebook and update. The online version is simply for convenience for those who do have access. If<L.31.1>
you really want a copy printed off and posted to you let me know, but there'll be a 0.5 credit charge to cover the costs.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>HowBaseballWorks.com <C> You should find a new website at www.howbaseballworks.com - it's intended to provide a guide to MLB,<L.31.1>
both for the inexperienced viewer, but also for the more experienced people (like you lot). It isn't just there to be interesting<L.31.1>
and informative, as sadly they don't pay the bills, so the hope is that traffic through it will produce Gameplan Baseball players!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
If you're on a chat forum (not one full of people already converted) then please give it a plug - remember that we offer a couple<L.31.1>
of free credits for anyone new you introduce to our games (which is for genuinely new punters, not people switching leagues) and<L.31.1>
it's in your interests to get new players (ie new competition as well). So if you know some baseball fans, give it a plug.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Websites <C> The website for submitting orders is at www.softsim.co.uk. www.pbmsports.com is our main "static" information<L.31.1>
website, as well as news of what's going on here. For news of what is happening with Pete in Yeovil see www.sidetracks.co.uk. For<L.31.1>
information on baseball and how it works, see www.howbaseballworks.com - a site also designed for recruiting new punters!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Internet Orders <C> Should be submitted online by 9am. The confirmation that they've been received by us is the page that comes<L.1.1>
<P>
<L>
<L.1.1>
up in response to you pushing the button. When you see that page, your orders are in. The version that's emailed to you is just<L.31.1>
for information - we email it to save you having to copy and paste or save it as a screenshot. If the email copy of your orders<L.31.1>
doesn't appear don't worry - emails get delayed or go missing quite often (far more than some people think). The more people who<L.31.1>
submit orders via the internet the better - if you want more information, just ask. You can also pay for credits online.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Email Results <C> Emailed results are normally sent out between 3pm and 6pm. If there's a delay in processing, it'll say so on<L.31.1>
www.pbmsports.com - please check there first. If you haven't received emailed results 24 hours after they're due, then email me<L.31.1>
and ask for them to be resent. Don't ask me before the 24 hours are due, but don't wait much longer either.  <L.31.1>
